* Senior club appearances and goals counted for the domestic league only&#32;and correct as of 13 February 2021<br />‡ National team caps and goals correct as of 14 October 2020</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Giorgio Chiellini</b> (<small>Italian pronunciation:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Italian" title="Help:IPA/Italian">[drdo kjellini, dor-]</a></span>; born 14 August 1984) is an Italian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)" title="Defender (association football)">defender</a> and <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captains</a> both <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> club <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy national team</a>. He is a physically strong and aggressive defender, and is considered one of the world's best <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre-back" title="Defender (association football)">centre-backs</a>; he is also capable of playing as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">left-back</a>, both in a three or four-man defence.
</p><p>At club level, Chiellini began his career with <a href="/wiki/A.S._Livorno_Calcio" title="A.S. Livorno Calcio">Livorno</a> in 2000, also later playing for <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a> and <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>, before moving to Juventus in 2005. With Juventus, he has won nine consecutive <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> titles from 2012 to 2020, as well as four consecutive <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> titles, and four <a href="/wiki/Supercoppa_Italiana" title="Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> titles. Chiellini has been named in the <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Team_of_the_Year" title="Serie A Team of the Year">Serie A Team of the Year</a> five times: in <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Team_of_the_Year#2012.E2.80.9313" title="Serie A Team of the Year">2012–13</a>, <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Team_of_the_Year#2014.E2.80.9315" title="Serie A Team of the Year">2014–15</a>, <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Team_of_the_Year#2015.E2.80.9316" title="Serie A Team of the Year">2015–16</a>, <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Team_of_the_Year#2017.E2.80.9318" title="Serie A Team of the Year">2017–18</a> and <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Team_of_the_Year#2018–19_Serie_A" title="Serie A Team of the Year">2018–19</a> and has been awarded the <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Defender_of_the_Year" title="Serie A Defender of the Year">Serie A Defender of the Year</a> also three times: in 2008, 2009 and 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:1_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:2_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Gran_Galà_del_calcio_-_2016_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Gran_Galà_del_calcio_-_2016-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He made his international debut for Italy in 2004, and currently has a total of 105 <a href="/wiki/Cap_(sport)" title="Cap (sport)">caps</a>, making him <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team_records#Appearances" class="mw-redirect" title="Italy national football team records">Italy's seventh-highest appearance holder</a>. He was selected in the nation's squads for the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2004_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2004 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2004 Olympics</a>, winning a bronze medal, as well as for three <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship" title="UEFA European Championship">UEFA European Championships</a>, two <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cups</a> and two <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="FIFA Confederations Cup">FIFA Confederations Cups</a>, helping the <i>Azzurri</i> to reach the final of <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a> and achieve a third-place finish at the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</a>.
</p>
