<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Livorno">Livorno</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Livorno">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Chiellini joined the youth teams at <a href="/wiki/A.S._Livorno_Calcio" title="A.S. Livorno Calcio">Livorno</a> at age six and started out as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>. As he matured, he switched to playing as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a> and finally he found his position as a left back. He played in the club's youth academy between 1990 and 2000, before earning first team call-ups for the 2000–01 <a href="/wiki/Serie_C1" class="mw-redirect" title="Serie C1">Serie C1</a> season. In his first season with the first team, Chiellini made three appearances and followed that up with five more appearances the following season.
</p><p>In June 2002, Chiellini was signed by <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Co-ownership_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Co-ownership (football)">co-ownership</a> deal, for €3.1 million, (who also saw <a href="/wiki/Marco_Amelia" title="Marco Amelia">Marco Amelia</a>, move in the opposite direction, for €2.8 million)<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> however, he was loaned back to Livorno for the <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_Serie_B" title="2002–03 Serie B">2002–03</a> <a href="/wiki/Serie_B" title="Serie B">Serie B</a> season, after they had earned promotion. In his first Serie B season, Chiellini made six seasonal appearances, also making his <a href="/wiki/Coppa_Italia" title="Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> debut. In his second Serie B season, Chiellini broke into the starting line-up for the club, and would go on to make 42 official appearances, also scoring four goals from his left back position.
</p><p>In June 2004, Livorno officially bought back Chiellini for €3 million.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> During his four-season spell with the clubs' first team, Chiellini made a total of 57 appearances, scoring four goals, before his transfer to Juventus.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fiorentina">Fiorentina</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Fiorentina">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Chiellini was signed by Juventus in the summer 2004 for €6.5 million from Livorno,<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> but was immediately sold in a co-ownership deal to <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a> for €3.5 million, and played on the Florentine team during the <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_Serie_A" title="2004–05 Serie A">2004–05</a> <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> season. The complex deal actually meant Juventus bought Roma's half for €3 million and Fiorentina bought Livorno's half for €3.5 million. In his loan season with the club, Chiellini was a regular in the club's starting XI, making 42 official appearances, also scoring three goals.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Juventus">Juventus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Juventus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2005.E2.80.932011:_Early_years.2C_Calciopoli_and_struggles"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2005–2011:_Early_years,_Calciopoli_and_struggles">2005–2011: Early years, Calciopoli and struggles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2005–2011: Early years, Calciopoli and struggles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Juventus_v_Chievo,_5_April_2009_-_Giorgio_Chiellini.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Juventus_v_Chievo%2C_5_April_2009_-_Giorgio_Chiellini.jpg/220px-Juventus_v_Chievo%2C_5_April_2009_-_Giorgio_Chiellini.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="349" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Juventus_v_Chievo%2C_5_April_2009_-_Giorgio_Chiellini.jpg/330px-Juventus_v_Chievo%2C_5_April_2009_-_Giorgio_Chiellini.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Juventus_v_Chievo%2C_5_April_2009_-_Giorgio_Chiellini.jpg/440px-Juventus_v_Chievo%2C_5_April_2009_-_Giorgio_Chiellini.jpg 2x" data-file-width="504" data-file-height="800" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Juventus_v_Chievo,_5_April_2009_-_Giorgio_Chiellini.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Chiellini with <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in 2009</div></div></div>
<p>After an excellent first season in Serie A, Chiellini was recalled for the <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_Serie_A" title="2005–06 Serie A">2005–06 season</a> and Juventus paid €4.3 million for the rest of his contract. He became a regular under <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Capello" title="Fabio Capello">Fabio Capello</a> and made 23 appearances in his first season with the club, also helping the <i>Old Lady</i> to their 29th <i><a href="/wiki/Scudetto" title="Scudetto">scudetto</a></i> (which was later assigned to <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter</a> following the <a href="/wiki/2006_Italian_football_scandal" class="mw-redirect" title="2006 Italian football scandal">2006 "Calciopoli" scandal</a>).
</p><p>While in the <a href="/wiki/Serie_B" title="Serie B">Serie B</a>, he started playing at centre back, partnering <a href="/wiki/Nicola_Legrottaglie" title="Nicola Legrottaglie">Nicola Legrottaglie</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jean-Alain_Boumsong" title="Jean-Alain Boumsong">Jean-Alain Boumsong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Robert_Kova%C4%8D" title="Robert Kova">Robert Kova</a> at various stages of the season. Juventus won the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_Serie_B" title="2006–07 Serie B">2006–07 Serie B</a> title, gaining Serie A promotion with the best goal difference, conceding only 30 goals and scoring over 80 in 42 matches. He scored a double in a 5–1 thrashing at <a href="/wiki/U.S._Arezzo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Arezzo">Arezzo</a> in May, a result that mathematically sealed promotion for Juventus.
</p><p>With Juventus back in Serie A for the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Serie_A" title="2007–08 Serie A">2007–08 season</a>, Chiellini again was a starter for the club at left back, but following injuries to <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Andrade" title="Jorge Andrade">Jorge Andrade</a> and <a href="/wiki/Domenico_Criscito" title="Domenico Criscito">Domenico Criscito</a>, he was shifted to centre back again. Chiellini had a tremendous season and eventually made the position his own. Alongside fellow centre-half Nicola Legrottaglie, the duo were instrumental as Juventus finished the season with the joint second-best defensive record. The surprising aspect of this is that neither were considered remotely close to pinning down a centre back position in the summer before the season, with Domenico Criscito and Jorge Andrade preferred as the starting duo. He has been a regular fixture in the Juventus backline since their return to Serie A and was notably named <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the match">Man of the Match</a> in a game against Juventus rivals, <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Internazionale</a> when he won a physical and heated duel with former teammate <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a>, keeping the <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Swedish</a> striker at bay. Chiellini extended his original contract from until 2009 to 2011 on 12 October 2006.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> On 27 April 2008, Chiellini scored twice for Juventus in 5–2 win over <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a> that confirmed Juventus's place in the Serie A top four.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> on 26 June 2008, Chiellini extended his contract with Juventus until 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Serie_A" title="2008–09 Serie A">2008–09 season</a>, Chiellini remained as first choice in central defence alongside Nicola Legrottaglie. Chiellini scored his first goal in <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">Europe</a> on 13 August 2008 as Juve beat <a href="/wiki/FC_Petr%C5%BEalka_akad%C3%A9mia" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Petržalka akadémia">Artmedia Petržalka</a> 4–0 in the first leg of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> third qualifying round tie.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he injured his left knee again during the <a href="/wiki/Trofeo_Luigi_Berlusconi" title="Trofeo Luigi Berlusconi">Trofeo Luigi Berlusconi</a> against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> and missed the start of the Serie A season,<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> returning to duty in September starting in each of Juve's first three Champions League group games. At the end of the year, he was named <a href="/wiki/Serie_A_Defender_of_the_Year" title="Serie A Defender of the Year">Serie A Defender of the Year</a> for 2008 at the annual <i><a href="/wiki/Gran_Gal%C3%A0_del_Calcio" title="Gran Galà del Calcio">Oscar del Calcio</a></i> awards ceremony. On 10 March 2009, Chiellini was sent off for a second bookable offense during the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2008–09 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League first knockout round</a> second leg tie at home in a tightly contested match against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, but Juventus were eliminated 3–2 on aggregate after holding the former English champions to a 2–2 draw.
</p><p>An injury sustained in the win over <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a> on 6 March 2010 sidelined him for several important games and, in his absence, Juventus embarked on a miserable run of form, conceding nine goals in the four games he missed.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He marked his return by scoring the opening goal away at <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a> but was unable to prevent Juventus from succumbing to a 3–1 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> On 23 November 2010, Chiellini extended his contract with Juventus again until 30 June 2015 and was given a pay raise.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Serie_A" title="2010–11 Serie A">2010–11 season</a>, Chiellini was mostly partnered with newly signed youngster <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_Bonucci" title="Leonardo Bonucci">Leonardo Bonucci</a>. With the arrival of fellow Italy international <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Barzagli" title="Andrea Barzagli">Andrea Barzagli</a> in the winter transfer window, Chiellini occasionally played at left back to accommodate the Bonucci-Barzagli partnership and sometimes partnered Barzagli.
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.932014:_First_scudetto_and_domestic_dominance"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2011–2014:_First_scudetto_and_domestic_dominance">2011–2014: First scudetto and domestic dominance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2011–2014: First scudetto and domestic dominance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Giorgio_Chiellini_(Juventus).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Giorgio_Chiellini_%28Juventus%29.jpg/250px-Giorgio_Chiellini_%28Juventus%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="260" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Giorgio_Chiellini_%28Juventus%29.jpg/375px-Giorgio_Chiellini_%28Juventus%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Giorgio_Chiellini_%28Juventus%29.jpg/500px-Giorgio_Chiellini_%28Juventus%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="546" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Giorgio_Chiellini_(Juventus).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Chiellini playing for the <i>Bianconeri</i> in 2012</div></div></div>
<p>Under manager <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Conte" title="Antonio Conte">Antonio Conte</a>, Chiellini returned to his original position at left back due to Barzagli and Bonucci's good run of form. After struggling to re-adapt back to his former position, he grew into his role and managed to keep <a href="/wiki/Paolo_De_Ceglie" title="Paolo De Ceglie">Paolo De Ceglie</a>, the only other natural left back in the squad, on the bench for much of the first half of the 2011–12 season. In the second half of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Serie_A" title="2011–12 Serie A">2011–12 season</a>, Conte switched to a three-man defence, where Chiellini partnered Bonucci and Barzagli in a very successful defensive system for Juve, who ended the season as Serie A champions, with the best defensive record, as well as being unbeaten in the league.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Due to their performances together, the three-man defence earned the nickname <i>BBC</i>, a reference to the players' initials,<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> and soon the trio established themselves as one of the best defences in world football during the following seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-opposition_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-opposition-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Juventus lost the <a href="/wiki/2012_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2012 Coppa Italia Final">2012 Coppa Italia Final</a> against <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a>, but would later defeat them in the <a href="/wiki/2012_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2012 Supercoppa Italiana">2012 Supercoppa Italiana</a>, although Chiellini would miss the match.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Chiellini made his 250th appearance with Juventus on 22 September 2012, on his first appearance of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Serie_A" title="2012–13 Serie A">2012–13 season</a> after coming back from injury, in a 2–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/A.C._ChievoVerona" title="A.C. ChievoVerona">Chievo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On 1 March 2013, after coming back from another injury suffered in mid-December, he scored a header in a 1–1 draw over Napoli at the San Paolo stadium, which allowed Juventus to keep their 6-point lead over Napoli, who were in second place.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Juventus retained the Serie A title and the <a href="/wiki/2013_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2013 Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> that season, once again finishing the year with the best defensive record in Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Chiellini was the only Italian player to be nominated for the 2013 <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 October 2013, Chiellini scored in Juventus's 3–2 win over Milan, scoring the match winning goal; the next day he announced the renewal of his contract with Juventus, which would keep him at the club until 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He made his 300th appearance with Juventus in a 3–0 Serie A victory against Roma on 5 January 2014,<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> as he went on to win his third consecutive <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Serie_A" title="2013–14 Serie A">league title</a> with Juventus that season.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.932018:_Continued_domestic_success_and_two_Champions_League_finals"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–2018:_Continued_domestic_success_and_two_Champions_League_finals">2014–2018: Continued domestic success and two Champions League finals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2014–2018: Continued domestic success and two Champions League finals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/2014_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2014 Supercoppa Italiana">2014 Supercoppa Italiana</a> on 22 December 2014, Juventus were defeated by Napoli on penalties after a 2–2 draw following extra-time; Chiellini missed one of Juventus's spot-kicks in the resulting shoot-out.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> On 20 May, Chiellini captained Juventus in the club's 2–1 win over Lazio in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2015 Coppa Italia Final">2015 Coppa Italia Final</a>, also scoring Juventus's first goal of the night.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 June 2015, it was confirmed that Chiellini would not participate in the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2015 UEFA Champions League Final">2015 UEFA Champions League Final</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> as a scan on his left leg revealed he had a first degree calf muscle tear.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>	In the absence of Chiellini, Juventus were defeated 3–1 by Barcelona at Berlin's <a href="/wiki/Olympiastadion_(Berlin)" title="Olympiastadion (Berlin)">Olympiastadion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Juventus_Coppa_Italia_2016.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Juventus_Coppa_Italia_2016.jpg/250px-Juventus_Coppa_Italia_2016.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="168" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Juventus_Coppa_Italia_2016.jpg/375px-Juventus_Coppa_Italia_2016.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Juventus_Coppa_Italia_2016.jpg/500px-Juventus_Coppa_Italia_2016.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="861" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Juventus_Coppa_Italia_2016.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Chiellini (center), Juventus' captain during the <a href="/wiki/2016_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2016 Coppa Italia Final">2016 Coppa Italia Final</a>, receives the trophy by the President of the Italian Republic, <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Mattarella" title="Sergio Mattarella">Sergio Mattarella</a> (right).</div></div></div>
<p>Chiellini was ruled out of the <a href="/wiki/2015_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2015 Supercoppa Italiana">2015 Supercoppa Italiana</a> after sustaining an injury in a 2–1 away friendly victory over <a href="/wiki/Lechia_Gda%C5%84sk" title="Lechia Gdask">Lechia Gdask</a> on 29 July, which kept him sidelined for three weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> On 24 November, Chiellini was nominated for the 2015 UEFA Team of the Year.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 February 2016, it was confirmed that Chiellini would miss the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Serie_A" title="2015–16 Serie A">Serie A</a> match on 13 February against <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a>, as well as the first round of 16 leg of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> on 23 February against <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> due to an injury.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Chiellini returned to action on 28 February to take on <a href="/wiki/Derby_d%27Italia" title="Derby d&#39;Italia">rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Internazionale</a>, yet again sustaining an injury to his thigh which caused him to limp off the pitch and substituted off in the 35th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-coppaitaliainjury_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-coppaitaliainjury-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> After already having missed the first round of 16 leg against Bayern, there was further doubt as to if he would miss the second leg as well on 16 March. However, after medical testing it was estimated he would only be out for ten days, initially thought to only miss the second leg of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Coppa_Italia" title="2015–16 Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia</a> semi-finals against Internazionale on 2 March and a Serie A match against <a href="/wiki/Atalanta_B.C." title="Atalanta B.C.">Atalanta</a> on 6 March;<sup id="cite_ref-coppaitaliainjury_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-coppaitaliainjury-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> he wouldn't be fit for the second round of 16 leg of the Champions League, and missed the match.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> He returned from injury on 2 April, starting in a 1–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Empoli_F.C." title="Empoli F.C.">Empoli</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> but sustained yet another injury to his <a href="/wiki/Adductor_longus_muscle" title="Adductor longus muscle">adductor longus muscle</a> in his right thigh before being substituted off in the 54th minute of that match; further tests in the following days revealed he would be out for 20 days.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> He returned to action once again in a 2–1 away defeat to <a href="/wiki/Hellas_Verona_F.C." title="Hellas Verona F.C.">Verona</a>, on 8 May.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> After constant injury spells throughout the season, Chiellini scored in the last match of the season on 14 May in the 77th minute of a 5–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a>, as Juventus celebrated winning the league title for a fifth consecutive time since the 2011–12 season; this was Chiellini's 400th appearance for Juventus.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> On 21 May, Chiellini captained Juventus in the <a href="/wiki/2016_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2016 Coppa Italia Final">2016 Coppa Italia Final</a> in Rome; he played a key role in a 1–0 extra-time victory over Milan (the club's eleventh Coppa Italia title in total), helping his team to defend the title and keep a clean sheet.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> He later lifted the trophy as Juventus became the first Italian club ever to win consecutive domestic doubles.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:33%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"It’s actually better to have Chiellini."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—In an interview with <i><a href="/wiki/Tuttosport" title="Tuttosport">Tuttosport</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Federico_Bernardeschi" title="Federico Bernardeschi">Federico Bernardeschi</a> underlined that despite <a href="/wiki/Transfer_of_Cristiano_Ronaldo_from_Real_Madrid_C.F._to_Juventus_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Transfer of Cristiano Ronaldo from Real Madrid C.F. to Juventus F.C.">the arrival</a> of <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>, everyone wanted Chiellini on their team in training games.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 26 October 2016, Chiellini scored two goals in a 4–1 home win over Sampdoria after three weeks out due to injury.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On 23 December, Chiellini scored the opening goal in the <a href="/wiki/2016_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2016 Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> against Milan, but it ended in defeat as Milan won 4–3 in penalty shoot-out following a 1–1 draw after extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 28 April, he made his 300th appearance in Serie A with Juventus in a 2–2 away draw against Atalanta.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> On 3 June, after Chiellini missed out on the 2015 Champions League Final, he started in the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2017 UEFA Champions League Final">2017 final</a>, Juventus' second final appearance in three years, but were defeated 4–1 by defending champions Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-Guardian_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 September 2017, Chiellini missed the opening <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">2017–18 Champions League</a> group stage match of the season against Barcelona, due to a calf injury.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 January 2018, Chiellini was named to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year#Team_of_the_Year_2017" title="UEFA Team of the Year">2017 UEFA Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-team2017_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-team2017-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> He made his 350th appearance in Serie A in a 0–0 away draw against <a href="/wiki/S.P.A.L._2013" class="mw-redirect" title="S.P.A.L. 2013">S.P.A.L.</a>, on 17 March.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.93present:_Juventus_captain_and_eighth_consecutive_Serie_A_title"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–present:_Juventus_captain_and_eighth_consecutive_Serie_A_title">2018–present: Juventus captain and eighth consecutive Serie A title</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2018–present: Juventus captain and eighth consecutive Serie A title">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 29 June 2018, Chiellini was given a two-year contract extension until 2020 and also named the club's new captain after the departure of Buffon.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini_to_become_Juve_captain_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini_to_become_Juve_captain-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 16 January 2019, Chiellini lifted his first title as Juventus's new official captain – the <a href="/wiki/2018_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2018 Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> – following a 1–0 victory over Milan.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> On 12 March, Chiellini marked his 500th appearance in a Juventus jersey with a 3–0 win home to <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">Champions League round of 16 second leg</a> to overturn a 2–0 deficit to reach the quarter-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Juventus ended the season as league champions, with Chiellini capturing his record eighth Serie A title with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 24 August, in Juventus's opening match of the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Juventus_F.C._season" title="2019–20 Juventus F.C. season">2019–20 season</a> against <a href="/wiki/Parma_Calcio_1913" title="Parma Calcio 1913">Parma</a>, Chiellini scored the only goal of the match in a 1–0 away win in Serie A.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On 30 August, Chiellini tore his <a href="/wiki/Anterior_cruciate_ligament" title="Anterior cruciate ligament">anterior cruciate ligament</a> during training.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> He returned on 16 February 2020, in a match against Brescia, replacing <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_Bonucci" title="Leonardo Bonucci">Leonardo Bonucci</a> in the 78th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> On 29 June, Chiellini signed a new contract with Juventus, extending until June 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 20 October 2020, Chiellini made his 71st Champions League appearance with Juventus in the team's opening European game of the season, a 2–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Dynamo_Kyiv" title="FC Dynamo Kyiv">Dynamo Kyiv</a>, overtaking <a href="/wiki/Alessio_Tacchinardi" title="Alessio Tacchinardi">Alessio Tacchinardi</a> as the club's third–most capped player of all time in the competition; however, he suffered an injury during the first half and was replaced by <a href="/wiki/Merih_Demiral" title="Merih Demiral">Merih Demiral</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="2000.E2.80.932008:_Youth_career.2C_early_senior_career_and_Euro_2008"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2000–2008:_Youth_career,_early_senior_career_and_Euro_2008">2000–2008: Youth career, early senior career and Euro 2008</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2000–2008: Youth career, early senior career and Euro 2008">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Chiellini represented Italy at all youth levels, and he won the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="UEFA European Under-19 Championship">European Under-19 Championship</a> with Italy in 2003,<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> and was also a member of the Italy team that won the bronze medal at the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2004_Summer_Olympics" title="Football at the 2004 Summer Olympics">football tournament</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2004_Summer_Olympics" title="2004 Summer Olympics">2004 Summer Olympics</a>. He participated in the <a href="/wiki/2006_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2006 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">2006</a> and 2007 U-21 Championships as Italy's captain, scoring 2 goals over both tournaments, although Italy were eliminated in the group stage on both occasions. He was named in the 'UEFA Team of the tournament' of the <a href="/wiki/2007_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2007 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">2007 U-21 Championships</a> held in the Netherlands,<sup id="cite_ref-giorgiochiellini.com_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-giorgiochiellini.com-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> where Italy also obtained qualification for the <a href="/wiki/2008_Summer_Olympics" title="2008 Summer Olympics">2008 Summer Olympics</a>. In total, he made 26 appearances for the Under-21 side, scoring 6 goals. 
</p><p>He made his debut for the <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italian national team</a> on 17 November 2004 against <a href="/wiki/Finland_national_football_team" title="Finland national football team">Finland</a> under <a href="/wiki/Marcello_Lippi" title="Marcello Lippi">Marcello Lippi</a>, at the age of 20.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> He became a regular squad member since 2007 and he scored his first goal for Italy on 21 November 2007, against the <a href="/wiki/Faroe_Islands_national_football_team" title="Faroe Islands national football team">Faroe Islands</a>, in <a href="/wiki/Modena" title="Modena">Modena</a>, in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2008 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2008 qualifying match</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Chiellini was called up to Italy's squad for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">UEFA Euro 2008</a> under manager <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Donadoni" title="Roberto Donadoni">Roberto Donadoni</a>, and injured captain <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Cannavaro" title="Fabio Cannavaro">Fabio Cannavaro</a> in a collision during a training session, that resulted in Cannavaro missing out on the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> He was sidelined in the opening game against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a>, which Italy went on to lose 3–0.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> He subsequently received the nod to partner <a href="/wiki/Christian_Panucci" title="Christian Panucci">Christian Panucci</a> at centre-back from the second game onwards, cementing his place in the <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team"><i>Azzurri</i></a> defence;<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> in the second group match of the tournament, he assisted Panucci's equaliser in a 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> While he also featured in the final group game, keeping a clean-sheet in a 2–0 win against <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> his most impressive display was arguably against <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> in the quarter-finals, where he famously neutralised the threat of the Spanish attacking duo of <a href="/wiki/David_Villa" title="David Villa">David Villa</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Torres" title="Fernando Torres">Fernando Torres</a>. The game ended 0–0, with Italy eventually losing 4–2 on <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalties</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2008.E2.80.932014:_European_Championship_runners-up"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2008–2014:_European_Championship_runners-up">2008–2014: European Championship runners-up</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 2008–2014: European Championship runners-up">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Chiellini_in_Nazionale.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Chiellini_in_Nazionale.jpg/250px-Chiellini_in_Nazionale.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Chiellini_in_Nazionale.jpg/375px-Chiellini_in_Nazionale.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Chiellini_in_Nazionale.jpg/500px-Chiellini_in_Nazionale.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="427" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Chiellini_in_Nazionale.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Chiellini with the Italian national team in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>During <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_8" title="2010 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Group 8">2010 World Cup qualifying</a>, Chiellini cemented his place as an undisputed first-choice in <a href="/wiki/Marcello_Lippi" title="Marcello Lippi">Marcello Lippi</a>'s squad. He played the full 90 minutes in all three group matches at the <a href="/wiki/2009_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2009 FIFA Confederations Cup">2009 FIFA Confederations Cup</a> but Italy were eliminated at the group stages on goal difference.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> He was also the starting Italy centre back, along with <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Cannavaro" title="Fabio Cannavaro">Cannavaro</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 World Cup</a>, although Italy disappointed and exited in the first round, finishing in last place in their group with two points, and failing to win a match or keep a clean sheet.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Under <a href="/wiki/Cesare_Prandelli" title="Cesare Prandelli">Cesare Prandelli</a>, Chiellini was once again the starting centre back during Italy's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying</a> campaign. Along with Juventus teammates <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Barzagli" title="Andrea Barzagli">Andrea Barzagli</a> and <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_Bonucci" title="Leonardo Bonucci">Leonardo Bonucci</a>, and also <a href="/wiki/Daniele_De_Rossi" title="Daniele De Rossi">Daniele De Rossi</a>, he started in defence for Italy in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a> tournament, after recovering from an injury he had encountered during the final Serie A game of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> He suffered another injury in Italy's final group match against <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Ireland</a>, which ended in a 2–0 win, ruling him out of the quarter-final fixture against <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-Italy&#39;s_Chiellini_to_miss_quarter-final_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Italy&#39;s_Chiellini_to_miss_quarter-final-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> he returned to the starting line-up for Italy's 2–1 semi-final victory over <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-infortunio_muscolare_per_Chiellini_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-infortunio_muscolare_per_Chiellini-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> Italy reached the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Final">final</a>, but were defeated once again by Spain, suffering a 4–0 loss. Despite suffering a minor injury in the semi-final, Chiellini started as left back in the final, but was substituted after sustaining yet another injury; Spain's first goal of the match arose from his mistake, due to his precarious physical condition.<sup id="cite_ref-infortunio_muscolare_per_Chiellini_83-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-infortunio_muscolare_per_Chiellini-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 14 November 2012, in a 2–1 friendly defeat to <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>, Chiellini wore the captain's armband with Italy for the first time in his career.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 June 2013, Chiellini scored his third goal for Italy against <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 Confederations Cup</a> in a 2–4 defeat, a low shot to the net after the referee <a href="/wiki/Ravshan_Irmatov" title="Ravshan Irmatov">Ravshan Irmatov</a> had initially signaled for a penalty kick to Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> Italy managed to finish the tournament in third place, following a 3–2 penalty shootout win over <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a> in the bronze medal match.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas_and_Giorgio_Chiellini_Euro_2012_final.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas_and_Giorgio_Chiellini_Euro_2012_final.jpg/250px-Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas_and_Giorgio_Chiellini_Euro_2012_final.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas_and_Giorgio_Chiellini_Euro_2012_final.jpg/375px-Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas_and_Giorgio_Chiellini_Euro_2012_final.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas_and_Giorgio_Chiellini_Euro_2012_final.jpg/500px-Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas_and_Giorgio_Chiellini_Euro_2012_final.jpg 2x" data-file-width="656" data-file-height="435" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas_and_Giorgio_Chiellini_Euro_2012_final.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Chiellini (right) challenges <a href="/wiki/Cesc_F%C3%A0bregas" title="Cesc Fàbregas">Cesc Fàbregas</a> of <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> during the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Final">UEFA Euro 2012 Final</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">2014 FIFA World Cup Qualifying</a> fixture against the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic_national_football_team" title="Czech Republic national football team">Czech Republic</a>, at the <a href="/wiki/Juventus_Stadium" title="Juventus Stadium">Juventus Stadium</a> in Turin, on 10 September 2013, Chiellini scored Italy's first goal in a 2–1 home win, which allowed the nation to clinch the top spot in their group and qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> in Brazil with two games at hand; this was the first time that the Italian squad had done so.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the 2014 World Cup, in Italy's final group stage game against Uruguay, replays showed <a href="/wiki/Luis_Su%C3%A1rez" title="Luis Suárez">Luis Suárez</a> biting Chiellini on the shoulder before Suárez fell and clutched his face, in Suárez's third career biting incident. As the Italian players protested to the Mexican referee <a href="/wiki/Marco_Antonio_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="Marco Antonio Rodríguez">Marco Antonio Rodríguez</a> for not penalizing Suárez, Uruguay won a corner and scored, winning 1–0 to qualify for the last 16 and eliminating Italy.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> As a result, the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Disciplinary_Code" title="FIFA Disciplinary Code">FIFA Disciplinary Committee</a> launched an investigation into the incident. On 26 June, The FIFA Disciplinary Committee announced that Suárez would be suspended for nine matches and banned from any football activity (including entering any stadium) for four months. Suárez was also fined <a href="/wiki/Swiss_franc" title="Swiss franc">CHF</a>100,000 (approx. <a href="/wiki/Pound_sterling" title="Pound sterling">£</a>65,700/<a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">€</a>82,000/<a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US$</a>119,000).<sup id="cite_ref-FIFABan_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFABan-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Luis_Suarez_suspended_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Luis_Suarez_suspended-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Even so, Chiellini expressed his view that the four-month ban for Suárez was "excessive".<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2014.E2.80.932016:_Euro_2016_campaign"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–2016:_Euro_2016_campaign">2014–2016: Euro 2016 campaign</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 2014–2016: Euro 2016 campaign">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 10 October 2014 in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan_national_football_team" title="Azerbaijan national football team">Azerbaijan</a> in <a href="/wiki/Palermo" title="Palermo">Palermo</a>, Chiellini put Italy ahead with a first-half header. He then scored a late own goal, but headed a winner three minutes from time to give Italy a 2–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> Italy qualified for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">Euro 2016</a> on 10 October of the following year after a 3–1 win over Azerbaijan.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> On 17 November 2015, Chiellini made his 82nd appearance for Italy in a 2–2 friendly home draw against Romania, overtaking <a href="/wiki/Franco_Baresi" title="Franco Baresi">Franco Baresi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Giuseppe_Bergomi" title="Giuseppe Bergomi">Giuseppe Bergomi</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Marco_Tardelli" title="Marco Tardelli">Marco Tardelli</a> as <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team_records#Appearances" class="mw-redirect" title="Italy national football team records">Italy's tenth most capped player of all time</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> On 31 May 2016, Chiellini was named to Conte's 23-man Italy squad for Euro 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> Playing alongside Bonucci and Barzagli, Chiellini drew praise for his defensive performances, as he helped Italy keep clean-sheets in both of their opening two victories over <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a>, which enabled the nation to top their group and advance to the second round.<sup id="cite_ref-opposition_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-opposition-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Having been booked for a tactical foul in Italy's opening match on 13 June,<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> Chiellini was rested for Italy's final group match against Ireland on 22 June, which ended in a 1–0 defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> In the round of 16 at <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a> in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> on 27 June, he scored the opening goal in a 2–0 win over reigning European champions Spain and helped Italy record their third clean-sheet of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> Italy were eliminated from the competition in a 6–5 penalty shoot-out defeat to reigning World Cup champions Germany in the quarter-finals, on 2 July.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2016.E2.80.932017:_2018_World_Cup_qualifying_campaign_and_retirement"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–2017:_2018_World_Cup_qualifying_campaign_and_retirement">2016–2017: 2018 World Cup qualifying campaign and retirement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2016–2017: 2018 World Cup qualifying campaign and retirement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In Italy's opening <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Israel_national_football_team" title="Israel national football team">Israel</a> on 5 September 2016, Chiellini earned his 90th international cap, but was later given his first ever national team red card after a second bookable offense in the 55th minute of an eventual 3–1 away win; causing him to miss the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_G" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Group G">next group match</a> against Spain on 6 October, an eventual 1–1 draw.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Chiellini also missed the return match against Spain on 2 September 2017, an eventual 3–0 away loss, as well as the return march against Israel on 5 September, an eventual 1–0 home win, with a calf injury.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> On 9 October, Chiellini made his 94th appearance for Italy in a 1–0 away victory over Albania in a World Cup qualifier, equalling <a href="/wiki/Giacinto_Facchetti" title="Giacinto Facchetti">Giacinto Facchetti</a> as <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team_records#Appearances" class="mw-redirect" title="Italy national football team records">the nation's joint-eighth highest appearance holder of all time</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> Italy finished in Group G in second place behind Spain, and advanced to the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Second_Round#Matches" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Second Round">play-off</a> against <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a>. Italy failed to qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> after a 1–0 aggregate loss to Sweden.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> Immediately following the second leg – a 0–0 home draw on 13 November –, was initially thought to be his final international appearance as Chiellini announced his retirement from the national team.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2018.E2.80.93present:_Return_and_captaincy"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–present:_Return_and_captaincy">2018–present: Return and captaincy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 2018–present: Return and captaincy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 17 March 2018, despite Chiellini's initial decision to retire, he was called up for the March 2018 friendlies against Argentina and England by interim manager <a href="/wiki/Luigi_Di_Biagio" title="Luigi Di Biagio">Luigi Di Biagio</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> After sustaining an injury, however, he was dropped from the squad, and <a href="/wiki/Angelo_Ogbonna" title="Angelo Ogbonna">Angelo Ogbonna</a> was called up in his place.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was once again called up to the national team in September 2018, by manager <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Mancini" title="Roberto Mancini">Roberto Mancini</a>, for Italy's opening <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Nations_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League</a> matches against <a href="/wiki/Poland_national_football_team" title="Poland national football team">Poland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> later that month.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> Chiellini was also named the new captain of the Italian national team following Gianluigi Buffon's international retirement.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> He subsequently wore the captain's armband in Italy's 1–1 home draw against Poland on 7 September, in their UEFA Nations League opener.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> On 11 October, he made his 98th appearance for Italy in a 1–1 friendly draw against <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_football_team" title="Ukraine national football team">Ukraine</a> in Genoa, equalling <a href="/wiki/Gianluca_Zambrotta" title="Gianluca Zambrotta">Gianluca Zambrotta</a> as his nation's joint-seventh highest appearance holder of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> On 17 November, he made his 100th appearance for Italy in a 0–0 draw against Portugal at the San Siro stadium in Milan, in his team's final UEFA Nations League match.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Drogba_ve_chiellini.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Drogba_ve_chiellini.JPG/220px-Drogba_ve_chiellini.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="251" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Drogba_ve_chiellini.JPG/330px-Drogba_ve_chiellini.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Drogba_ve_chiellini.JPG/440px-Drogba_ve_chiellini.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1518" data-file-height="1734" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Drogba_ve_chiellini.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Chiellini defending <a href="/wiki/Didier_Drogba" title="Didier Drogba">Didier Drogba</a> in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>Chiellini began his professional career as a defensive-minded <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">left-back</a>, but later made his name as an aggressive, courageous, physical, and hard-tackling <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre_back" title="Defender (association football)">centre-back</a>, with a penchant for scoring headers from set-pieces, due to his height, aerial prowess, athleticism, and strength. A versatile, consistent, commanding, and dependable left-footed defender, with good awareness, positional sense, and an ability to read the game, he is capable of playing both in a three or four-man defence.<sup id="cite_ref-Italy&#39;s_Chiellini_to_miss_quarter-final_82-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Italy&#39;s_Chiellini_to_miss_quarter-final-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Italy_profile_–_Giorgio_Chiellini_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Italy_profile_–_Giorgio_Chiellini-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini,_si_parte_All&#39;Europeo_ci_sei_120-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini,_si_parte_All&#39;Europeo_ci_sei-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Qual_è_il_ruolo_di_Giorgio_Chiellini?_121-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Qual_è_il_ruolo_di_Giorgio_Chiellini?-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini,_contrasti_duri_e_goal_importanti_122-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini,_contrasti_duri_e_goal_importanti-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_players_at_Euro_2016_123-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_players_at_Euro_2016-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-temperament_124-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-temperament-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Italy’s_World_Cup_23_125-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Italy’s_World_Cup_23-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-How_to_Defend_126-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_to_Defend-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> A hard-working player, he is also known for his ability to cover ground and put pressure on or anticipate opponents in positions higher up on the pitch.<sup id="cite_ref-temperament_124-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-temperament-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-How_to_Defend_126-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_to_Defend-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_centre-back_131-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_centre-back-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Italian_job_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Italian_job-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Regarded as a promising defender in his youth,<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> he came to be considered as one of the best defenders in world football,<sup id="cite_ref-Ten_of_the_Best_Defenders_in_the_World_135-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ten_of_the_Best_Defenders_in_the_World-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_centre-back_131-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_centre-back-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> one of the greatest defenders of his generation,<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> and one of Juventus's greatest defenders ever.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, his Juventus manager at the time –&#160;<a href="/wiki/Massimiliano_Allegri" title="Massimiliano Allegri">Massimiliano Allegri</a> – described him as "the best defender in the world."<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> Regarding Chiellini's strength and man-marking ability, his former Livorno manager <a href="/wiki/Walter_Mazzarri" title="Walter Mazzarri">Walter Mazzarri</a> once labeled him as "a force of nature", also adding "he's a universal player that any coach would love to have on his team.<sup id="cite_ref-La_società_sa_cosa_voglio_142-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-La_società_sa_cosa_voglio-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> He is from another planet; he can mark three players by himself."<sup id="cite_ref-Italy_profile_–_Giorgio_Chiellini_119-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Italy_profile_–_Giorgio_Chiellini-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini_è_di_un_altro_pianeta_143-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini_è_di_un_altro_pianeta-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his tenacious, no-nonsense playing style, Chiellini has been described as an "old-fashioned" centre-back, who primarily serves as a ball-winner;<sup id="cite_ref-How_to_Defend_126-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_to_Defend-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> his physicality and aggression as a defender, as well as his trademark <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">goal celebration</a>, which involves him beating his chest, have earned him the nickname "<a href="/wiki/King_Kong" title="King Kong">King Kong</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-temperament_124-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-temperament-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ultimouomo_148-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ultimouomo-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> Although he is not particularly skilful or elegant from a technical standpoint,<sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini,_si_parte_All&#39;Europeo_ci_sei_120-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini,_si_parte_All&#39;Europeo_ci_sei-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Italian_job_132-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Italian_job-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini&#39;s_leadership_149-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini&#39;s_leadership-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_Ramos_is_the_best_centre-back_in_the_world_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio_Ramos_is_the_best_centre-back_in_the_world-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Defenders_are_pessimistic_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defenders_are_pessimistic-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Ero_quello_scarso_e_bruttino_153-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ero_quello_scarso_e_bruttino-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ultimouomo_148-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ultimouomo-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup> he possesses good vision<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> and reliable distribution, which allows him to play the ball out or launch attacks from the back after winning back possession.<sup id="cite_ref-How_to_Defend_126-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-How_to_Defend-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A popular figure with fans, he is also known for his dedication and vocal leadership on the pitch, and was Juventus's long-time <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)#Vice-captain" title="Captain (association football)">vice captain</a>, behind <a href="/wiki/Gianluigi_Buffon" title="Gianluigi Buffon">Gianluigi Buffon</a>; following Buffon's departure in 2018, Chiellini was appointed the team's new <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini_to_become_Juve_captain_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini_to_become_Juve_captain-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Italian_job_132-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Italian_job-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini&#39;s_leadership_149-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini&#39;s_leadership-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> Although he is not known for his pace over short distances,<sup id="cite_ref-Sergio_Ramos_is_the_best_centre-back_in_the_world_151-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sergio_Ramos_is_the_best_centre-back_in_the_world-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Defenders_are_pessimistic_152-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defenders_are_pessimistic-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> he is also a mobile defender.<sup id="cite_ref-Ero_quello_scarso_e_bruttino_153-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ero_quello_scarso_e_bruttino-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> Moreover, he possesses a strong mentality, good temperament under pressure, determination, and excellent concentration, as well as an ability to organise his back-line.<sup id="cite_ref-Chiellini,_si_parte_All&#39;Europeo_ci_sei_120-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Chiellini,_si_parte_All&#39;Europeo_ci_sei-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-temperament_124-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-temperament-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> Despite his ability as a defender, he has often struggled with injuries in recent seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Chiellini was raised in <a href="/wiki/Livorno" title="Livorno">Livorno</a><sup id="cite_ref-temperament_124-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-temperament-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> and is one of twin boys.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> He completed a <i><a href="/wiki/Laurea" title="Laurea">laurea</a></i> (bachelor's degree) in economics and commerce at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Turin" title="University of Turin">University of Turin</a> in July 2010,<sup id="cite_ref-temperament_124-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-temperament-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> and earned a <i><a href="/wiki/Laurea#Second_cycle:_Laurea_Magistrale" title="Laurea">laurea magistrale</a></i> (<a href="/wiki/Master_of_Business_Administration" title="Master of Business Administration">master's degree) in business administration</a> in April 2017 from the same institution, graduating <i><a href="/wiki/Cum_laude" class="mw-redirect" title="Cum laude">cum laude</a></i> (with honours).<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> Chiellini is able to speak <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In July 2014, Chiellini married his long-time girlfriend Carolina Bonistalli at a private <a href="/wiki/Catholicism" class="mw-redirect" title="Catholicism">Catholic</a> ceremony at the <a href="/wiki/Sanctuary_of_Montenero" title="Sanctuary of Montenero">Sanctuary of Montenero</a> in <a href="/wiki/Livorno" title="Livorno">Livorno</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> The couple have two daughters: Nina born July 2015, and Olivia born June 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> That same year, he published a book, <i>C'è un angelo bianconero. Il mio maestro si chiama <a href="/wiki/Gaetano_Scirea" title="Gaetano Scirea">Scirea</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-treccani_177-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-treccani-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Chiellini features in <a href="/wiki/EA_Sports" title="EA Sports">EA Sports'</a> <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i> video game series</a>; he was on the covers of the Italian editions of <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_10" title="FIFA 10">FIFA 10</a></i>, alongside global cover star <a href="/wiki/Ronaldinho" title="Ronaldinho">Ronaldinho</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> and <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_11" title="FIFA 11">FIFA 11</a></i>, alongside global cover star <a href="/wiki/Kak%C3%A1" title="Kaká">Kaká</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Throughout the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Juventus_F.C._season" title="2017–18 Juventus F.C. season">2017–18 season</a>, Chiellini appeared in the <a href="/wiki/Netflix" title="Netflix">Netflix</a> <a href="/wiki/Docu-series" class="mw-redirect" title="Docu-series">docu-series</a> called <i><a href="/wiki/First_Team:_Juventus" title="First Team: Juventus">First Team: Juventus</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Corsa_180-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Corsa-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2020, Chiellini released his autobiography <i>Io, Giorgio</i>, with the profits going to the <i>insuperabili</i> charity during the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Italy" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Italy">COVID-19 pandemic in Italy</a>. However, Chiellini attracted controversy due to his strong criticism of his former club and international teammates <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Melo" title="Felipe Melo">Felipe Melo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mario_Balotelli" title="Mario Balotelli">Mario Balotelli</a> in his book.<sup id="cite_ref-treccani_177-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-treccani-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-row_182-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-row-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honours">Honours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Giorgio_Chiellini&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Honours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><b>Livorno</b><sup id="cite_ref-giorgiochiellini.com_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-giorgiochiellini.com-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>

<p><b>Juventus</b><sup id="cite_ref-giorgiochiellini.com_69-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-giorgiochiellini.com-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SW_183-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SW-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup>
